Top Extended Deck Lists
=======================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on December 12, 2010 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast










Listed below are all lists from Day 3 at Worlds which recorded 13 or more points in the six rounds of Extended.
